---
title: "Experiments Recordings"
description: "Update the Notion table with best scores and steps per benchmark from W&B runs, combining same-named runs and averaging available metrics."
---

<Columns cols={2}>
  <Card title="MCP Server" icon="cloud">
    notion, wandb, terminal, filesystem
  </Card>
  <Card title="Local Tool" icon="terminal">
    claim_done, python_execute, handle_overlong_tool_outputs
  </Card>
</Columns>

## Instruction

In the table of the Notion page `mcp_experiments_recordings`, based on the historical experiments of W&B project `mbzuai-llm/Guru`, list the highest val-core acc mean@1/mean@k scores for each benchmark according to the table headers, and calculate and fill in the Best Step for that run (format: step(average acc)).

Instructions:

- If multiple runs have the same name, treat them as one run for combined statistics.
- The average score should only be calculated using the arithmetic mean of metrics available at that step; missing metrics are not included.
- Only operate on the target page under the specified parent page; do not change column names or order.

```json
	 entityName: $entity) {\n        runs(first: 20) {\n            edges {\n                node {\n                    id\n                    name\n                    displayName\n                    state\n                    createdAt\n                    summaryMetrics\n                    historyKeys\n                }\n            }\n            pageInfo {\n                endCursor\n                hasNextPage\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}",
	 "variables": {"entity":"mbzuai-llm",
	"project":"Guru"}
}
```

```python 
import json

# Load the full data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/CcQ8rjmxcSCfeUA2Ad9avG.json', 'r') as f:
    data = json.load(f)

# Extract just the runs data
runs = data['project']['runs']['edges']
print(f"Total runs: {len(runs)}")

# Get basic info about each run
for i, run in enumerate(runs):
    node = run['node']
    print(f"\nRun {i+1}:")
    print(f"  ID: {node['name']}")
    print(f"  Display Name: {node['displayName']}")
    print(f"  State: {node['state']}")
    
    # Parse summary metrics to see what validation metrics are available
    summary = json.loads(node['summaryMetrics'])
    val_core_metrics = [k for k in summary.keys() if k.startswith('val-core/') and k.endswith('/acc/mean@1')]
    print(f"  Val-core metrics: {len(val_core_metrics)}")
    if len(val_core_metrics) <= 5:
        for metric in val_core_metrics:
            print(f"    {metric}: {summary[metric]}")
    else:
        print(f"    First 5: {val_core_metrics[:5]}")
```

```python 
import json

# Load the full data from the overlong output
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/CcQ8rjmxcSCfeUA2Ad9avG.json', 'r') as f:
    full_data = json.load(f)

# The data is wrapped in a "text" field
runs_data = json.loads(full_data['text'])
runs = runs_data['project']['runs']['edges']

print(f"Total runs: {len(runs)}")

# Get basic info about each run
for i, run in enumerate(runs):
    node = run['node']
    print(f"\nRun {i+1}:")
    print(f"  ID: {node['name']}")
    print(f"  Display Name: {node['displayName']}")
    print(f"  State: {node['state']}")
    
    # Parse summary metrics to see what validation metrics are available
    summary = json.loads(node['summaryMetrics'])
    val_core_metrics = [k for k in summary.keys() if k.startswith('val-core/') and k.endswith('/acc/mean@1')]
    print(f"  Val-core metrics: {len(val_core_metrics)}")
    if len(val_core_metrics) <= 5:
        for metric in val_core_metrics:
            print(f"    {metric}: {summary[metric]}")
    else:
        print(f"    First 5: {val_core_metrics[:5]}")
        
    # Also check for best@k metrics like AIME and AMC
    best_metrics = [k for k in summary.keys() if k.startswith('val-core/') and 'best@' in k]
    if best_metrics:
        print(f"  Best@k metrics: {len(best_metrics)}")
        for metric in best_metrics[:3]:
            print(f"    {metric}: {summary[metric]}")
```

```python 
import json

# Load the runs data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/CcQ8rjmxcSCfeUA2Ad9avG.json', 'r') as f:
    full_data = json.load(f)

runs_data = json.loads(full_data['text'])
runs = runs_data['project']['runs']['edges']

# Mapping from Notion table columns to W&B metric names
notion_to_wb_mapping = {
    'CodeIO': 'val-core/simulation__codeio/acc/mean@1',
    'HiTab': 'val-core/table__hitab/acc/mean@1',
    'SuperGPQA': 'val-core/stem__supergpqa/acc/mean@1',
    'LiveCodeBench': 'val-core/codegen__livecodebench/acc/mean@1',
    'AIME (8x)': 'val-core/math__aime_repeated_8x/acc/best@8/mean',
    'Ordering Puzzle': 'val-core/logic__ordering_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1',
    'HumanEval': 'val-core/codegen__humaneval/acc/mean@1',
    'Graph Logical': 'val-core/logic__graph_logical_dataset/acc/mean@1',
    'MultiHiertt': 'val-core/table__multihier/acc/mean@1',
    'ArcAgI1': 'val-core/simulation__arcagi1/acc/mean@1',
    'MBPP': 'val-core/codegen__mbpp/acc/mean@1',
    'Zebra Puzzle': 'val-core/logic__zebra_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1',
    'MATH': 'val-core/math__math/acc/mean@1',
    'GPQA': 'val-core/stem__gpqa/acc/mean@1',
    'AMC (4x)': 'val-core/math__amc_repeated_4x/acc/best@4/mean'
}

# Process each run and extract the final validation metrics
run_results = {}

for run in runs:
    node = run['node']
    run_name = node['displayName']
    run_id = node['name']
    state = node['state']
    
    if run_name not in run_results:
        run_results[run_name] = {
            'run_ids': [],
            'metrics': {},
            'steps': {},
            'states': []
        }
    
    run_results[run_name]['run_ids'].append(run_id)
    run_results[run_name]['states'].append(state)
    
    # Parse summary metrics
    summary = json.loads(node['summaryMetrics'])
    current_step = summary.get('_step', 0)
    
    # Extract metrics for each column
    for notion_col, wb_metric in notion_to_wb_mapping.items():
        if wb_metric in summary:
            value = summary[wb_metric]
            
            # Track the best value and step for this metric
            if notion_col not in run_results[run_name]['metrics']:
                run_results[run_name]['metrics'][notion_col] = []
                run_results[run_name]['steps'][notion_col] = []
            
            run_results[run_name]['metrics'][notion_col].append(value)
            run_results[run_name]['steps'][notion_col].append(current_step)

# Print summary
print("Run Results Summary:")
print("=" * 50)

for run_name, data in run_results.items():
    print(f"\nRun: {run_name}")
    print(f"  Run IDs: {data['run_ids']}")
    print(f"  States: {data['states']}")
    print(f"  Available metrics: {list(data['metrics'].keys())}")
    
    # Show best values for each metric
    for metric, values in data['metrics'].items():
        if values:
            best_idx = values.index(max(values))
            best_value = values[best_idx]
            best_step = data['steps'][metric][best_idx]
            print(f"    {metric}: {best_value:.4f} at step {best_step}")
```
</div>

```python 
import json

# Load the runs data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/CcQ8rjmxcSCfeUA2Ad9avG.json', 'r') as f:
    full_data = json.load(f)

runs_data = json.loads(full_data['text'])
runs = runs_data['project']['runs']['edges']

# Mapping from Notion table columns to W&B metric names
notion_to_wb_mapping = {
    'CodeIO': 'val-core/simulation__codeio/acc/mean@1',
    'HiTab': 'val-core/table__hitab/acc/mean@1',
    'SuperGPQA': 'val-core/stem__supergpqa/acc/mean@1',
    'LiveCodeBench': 'val-core/codegen__livecodebench/acc/mean@1',
    'AIME (8x)': 'val-core/math__aime_repeated_8x/acc/best@8/mean',
    'Ordering Puzzle': 'val-core/logic__ordering_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1',
    'HumanEval': 'val-core/codegen__humaneval/acc/mean@1',
    'Graph Logical': 'val-core/logic__graph_logical_dataset/acc/mean@1',
    'MultiHiertt': 'val-core/table__multihier/acc/mean@1',
    'ArcAgI1': 'val-core/simulation__arcagi1/acc/mean@1',
    'MBPP': 'val-core/codegen__mbpp/acc/mean@1',
    'Zebra Puzzle': 'val-core/logic__zebra_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1',
    'MATH': 'val-core/math__math/acc/mean@1',
    'GPQA': 'val-core/stem__gpqa/acc/mean@1',
    'AMC (4x)': 'val-core/math__amc_repeated_4x/acc/best@4/mean'
}

# First, let's get all data points for each run name and step
run_data_by_step = {}

for run in runs:
    node = run['node']
    run_name = node['displayName']
    run_id = node['name']
    state = node['state']
    
    if run_name not in run_data_by_step:
        run_data_by_step[run_name] = {}
    
    # Parse summary metrics
    summary = json.loads(node['summaryMetrics'])
    current_step = summary.get('_step', 0)
    
    if current_step not in run_data_by_step[run_name]:
        run_data_by_step[run_name][current_step] = {}
    
    # Extract metrics for each column
    for notion_col, wb_metric in notion_to_wb_mapping.items():
        if wb_metric in summary:
            value = summary[wb_metric]
            run_data_by_step[run_name][current_step][notion_col] = value

# Now find the best step for each run based on average accuracy
final_results = {}

for run_name, steps_data in run_data_by_step.items():
    print(f"\nProcessing run: {run_name}")
    
    best_step = None
    best_avg_acc = -1
    best_metrics = {}
    
    # For each step, calculate the average accuracy of available metrics
    for step, metrics in steps_data.items():
        if metrics:  # Only consider steps with metrics
            avg_acc = sum(metrics.values()) / len(metrics)
            print(f"  Step {step}: {len(metrics)} metrics, avg = {avg_acc:.4f}")
            
            if avg_acc > best_avg_acc:
                best_avg_acc = avg_acc
                best_step = step
                best_metrics = metrics.copy()
    
    if best_step is not None:
        final_results[run_name] = {
            'best_step': best_step,
            'best_avg_acc': best_avg_acc,
            'metrics': best_metrics
        }
        print(f"  ‚Üí Best step: {best_step} (avg acc: {best_avg_acc:.4f})")

print("\n" + "="*60)
print("FINAL RESULTS FOR NOTION TABLE:")
print("="*60)

for run_name, data in final_results.items():
    print(f"\nRun: {run_name}")
    print(f"Best Step: {data['best_step']} (avg acc: {data['best_avg_acc']:.4f})")
    print("Metrics:")
    for metric, value in data['metrics'].items():
        print(f"  {metric}: {value:.4f}")
```

```python 
import json

# Load the W&B data from the file
with open("/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/e9AUyeypZtyjjHpo6aWhiT.json", "r") as f:
    wandb_data = json.load(f)

# The actual data is nested inside the JSON
wandb_runs = json.loads(wandb_data["text"])["project"]["runs"]["edges"]

# Group runs by displayName
runs_by_name = {}
for run_edge in wandb_runs:
    run = run_edge["node"]
    display_name = run["displayName"]
    if display_name not in runs_by_name:
        runs_by_name[display_name] = []
    runs_by_name[display_name].append(run)

# Define the mapping from Notion column names to W&B metric keys
benchmark_mapping = {
    "CodeIO": "val-core/simulation__codeio/acc/mean@1",
    "HiTab": "val-core/table__hitab/acc/mean@1",
    "SuperGPQA": "val-core/stem__supergpqa/acc/mean@1",
    "LiveCodeBench": "val-core/codegen__livecodebench/acc/mean@1",
    "AIME (8x)": "val-core/math__aime_repeated_8x/acc/best@8/mean",
    "Ordering Puzzle": "val-core/logic__ordering_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "HumanEval": "val-core/codegen__humaneval/acc/mean@1",
    "Graph Logical": "val-core/logic__graph_logical_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "MultiHiertt": "val-core/table__multihier/acc/mean@1",
    "ArcAgI1": "val-core/simulation__arcagi1/acc/mean@1",
    "MBPP": "val-core/codegen__mbpp/acc/mean@1",
    "Zebra Puzzle": "val-core/logic__zebra_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "MATH": "val-core/math__math/acc/mean@1",
    "GPQA": "val-core/stem__gpqa/acc/mean@1",
    "AMC (4x)": "val-core/math__amc_repeated_4x/acc/best@4/mean",
}

results = {}

for run_name, runs in runs_by_name.items():
    best_scores = {bm: -1 for bm in benchmark_mapping.keys()}
    best_step_avg = -1
    best_step_str = ""

    for run in runs:
        try:
            summary_metrics = json.loads(run["summaryMetrics"])
            step = summary_metrics.get("_step", 0)
            current_avg = 0
            count = 0
            for notion_col, wandb_key in benchmark_mapping.items():
                if wandb_key in summary_metrics:
                    score = summary_metrics[wandb_key]
                    if score > best_scores[notion_col]:
                        best_scores[notion_col] = score
                    current_avg += score
                    count += 1
            if count > 0:
                current_avg /= count
                if current_avg > best_step_avg:
                    best_step_avg = current_avg
                    best_step_str = f"{step}({current_avg:.4f})"
        except (json.JSONDecodeError, TypeError):
            continue

    results[run_name] = {
        "scores": best_scores,
        "best_step": best_step_str,
    }

print(json.dumps(results, indent=2))
```

```python 

import json

# Load the W&B data from the file
with open("/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/e9AUyeypZtyjjHpo6aWhiT.json", "r") as f:
    wandb_data = json.load(f)

# The actual data is nested inside the JSON
wandb_runs = json.loads(json.loads(wandb_data["text"])['text'])["project"]["runs"]["edges"]

# Group runs by displayName
runs_by_name = {}
for run_edge in wandb_runs:
    run = run_edge["node"]
    display_name = run["displayName"]
    if display_name not in runs_by_name:
        runs_by_name[display_name] = []
    runs_by_name[display_name].append(run)

# Define the mapping from Notion column names to W&B metric keys
benchmark_mapping = {
    "CodeIO": "val-core/simulation__codeio/acc/mean@1",
    "HiTab": "val-core/table__hitab/acc/mean@1",
    "SuperGPQA": "val-core/stem__supergpqa/acc/mean@1",
    "LiveCodeBench": "val-core/codegen__livecodebench/acc/mean@1",
    "AIME (8x)": "val-core/math__aime_repeated_8x/acc/best@8/mean",
    "Ordering Puzzle": "val-core/logic__ordering_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "HumanEval": "val-core/codegen__humaneval/acc/mean@1",
    "Graph Logical": "val-core/logic__graph_logical_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "MultiHiertt": "val-core/table__multihier/acc/mean@1",
    "ArcAgI1": "val-core/simulation__arcagi1/acc/mean@1",
    "MBPP": "val-core/codegen__mbpp/acc/mean@1",
    "Zebra Puzzle": "val-core/logic__zebra_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "MATH": "val-core/math__math/acc/mean@1",
    "GPQA": "val-core/stem__gpqa/acc/mean@1",
    "AMC (4x)": "val-core/math__amc_repeated_4x/acc/best@4/mean",
}

results = {}

for run_name, runs in runs_by_name.items():
    best_scores = {bm: -1 for bm in benchmark_mapping.keys()}
    best_step_avg = -1
    best_step_str = ""

    for run in runs:
        try:
            summary_metrics = json.loads(run["summaryMetrics"])
            step = summary_metrics.get("_step", 0)
            current_avg = 0
            count = 0
            for notion_col, wandb_key in benchmark_mapping.items():
                if wandb_key in summary_metrics:
                    score = summary_metrics[wandb_key]
                    if score > best_scores[notion_col]:
                        best_scores[notion_col] = score
                    current_avg += score
                    count += 1
            if count > 0:
                current_avg /= count
                if current_avg > best_step_avg:
                    best_step_avg = current_avg
                    best_step_str = f"{step}({current_avg:.4f})"
        except (json.JSONDecodeError, TypeError):
            continue

    results[run_name] = {
        "scores": best_scores,
        "best_step": best_step_str,
    }

# Now, let's query the Notion database to get the page IDs for each run
database_id = "0a16773d-6317-4aa4-8709-7e155588b82a"

print(json.dumps(results, indent=2))


```

```python 

import json

# Load the W&B data from the file
with open("/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/e9AUyeypZtyjjHpo6aWhiT.json", "r") as f:
    wandb_data = json.load(f)

# The actual data is nested inside the JSON
wandb_runs = json.loads(json.loads(wandb_data["text"])['text'])["project"]["runs"]["edges"]

# Group runs by displayName
runs_by_name = {}
for run_edge in wandb_runs:
    run = run_edge["node"]
    display_name = run["displayName"]
    if display_name not in runs_by_name:
        runs_by_name[display_name] = []
    runs_by_name[display_name].append(run)

# Define the mapping from Notion column names to W&B metric keys
benchmark_mapping = {
    "CodeIO": "val-core/simulation__codeio/acc/mean@1",
    "HiTab": "val-core/table__hitab/acc/mean@1",
    "SuperGPQA": "val-core/stem__supergpqa/acc/mean@1",
    "LiveCodeBench": "val-core/codegen__livecodebench/acc/mean@1",
    "AIME (8x)": "val-core/math__aime_repeated_8x/acc/best@8/mean",
    "Ordering Puzzle": "val-core/logic__ordering_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "HumanEval": "val-core/codegen__humaneval/acc/mean@1",
    "Graph Logical": "val-core/logic__graph_logical_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "MultiHiertt": "val-core/table__multihier/acc/mean@1",
    "ArcAgI1": "val-core/simulation__arcagi1/acc/mean@1",
    "MBPP": "val-core/codegen__mbpp/acc/mean@1",
    "Zebra Puzzle": "val-core/logic__zebra_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "MATH": "val-core/math__math/acc/mean@1",
    "GPQA": "val-core/stem__gpqa/acc/mean@1",
    "AMC (4x)": "val-core/math__amc_repeated_4x/acc/best@4/mean",
}

results = {}

for run_name, runs in runs_by_name.items():
    best_scores = {bm: -1 for bm in benchmark_mapping.keys()}
    best_step_avg = -1
    best_step_str = ""

    for run in runs:
        try:
            summary_metrics = json.loads(run["summaryMetrics"])
            step = summary_metrics.get("_step", 0)
            current_avg = 0
            count = 0
            for notion_col, wandb_key in benchmark_mapping.items():
                if wandb_key in summary_metrics:
                    score = summary_metrics[wandb_key]
                    if score > best_scores[notion_col]:
                        best_scores[notion_col] = score
                    current_avg += score
                    count += 1
            if count > 0:
                current_avg /= count
                if current_avg > best_step_avg:
                    best_step_avg = current_avg
                    best_step_str = f"{step}({current_avg:.4f})"
        except (json.JSONDecodeError, TypeError):
            continue

    results[run_name] = {
        "scores": best_scores,
        "best_step": best_step_str,
    }


for run_name, data in results.items():
    properties = {
        "Run Name": {"title": [{"text": {"content": run_name}}]},
        "Best Step (Average)": {"rich_text": [{"text": {"content": data["best_step"]}}]}
    
    for benchmark, score in data["scores"].items():
        if score != -1:
            properties[benchmark] = {"number": score}

    print(f"Adding page for {run_name}")
    #notion_API_post_page(
    #    parent=notion_API_post_page.NotionApiPostPageParent(database_id="0a16773d-6317-4aa4-8709-7e155588b82a"),
    #    properties=properties
    #)
```

```python 

import json

# Load the W&B data from the file
with open("/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/e9AUyeypZtyjjHpo6aWhiT.json", "r") as f:
    wandb_data = json.load(f)

# The actual data is nested inside the JSON
wandb_runs = json.loads(json.loads(wandb_data["text"])['text'])["project"]["runs"]["edges"]

# Group runs by displayName
runs_by_name = {}
for run_edge in wandb_runs:
    run = run_edge["node"]
    display_name = run["displayName"]
    if display_name not in runs_by_name:
        runs_by_name[display_name] = []
    runs_by_name[display_name].append(run)

# Define the mapping from Notion column names to W&B metric keys
benchmark_mapping = {
    "CodeIO": "val-core/simulation__codeio/acc/mean@1",
    "HiTab": "val-core/table__hitab/acc/mean@1",
    "SuperGPQA": "val-core/stem__supergpqa/acc/mean@1",
    "LiveCodeBench": "val-core/codegen__livecodebench/acc/mean@1",
    "AIME (8x)": "val-core/math__aime_repeated_8x/acc/best@8/mean",
    "Ordering Puzzle": "val-core/logic__ordering_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "HumanEval": "val-core/codegen__humaneval/acc/mean@1",
    "Graph Logical": "val-core/logic__graph_logical_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "MultiHiertt": "val-core/table__multihier/acc/mean@1",
    "ArcAgI1": "val-core/simulation__arcagi1/acc/mean@1",
    "MBPP": "val-core/codegen__mbpp/acc/mean@1",
    "Zebra Puzzle": "val-core/logic__zebra_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "MATH": "val-core/math__math/acc/mean@1",
    "GPQA": "val-core/stem__gpqa/acc/mean@1",
    "AMC (4x)": "val-core/math__amc_repeated_4x/acc/best@4/mean",
}

results = {}

for run_name, runs in runs_by_name.items():
    best_scores = {bm: -1 for bm in benchmark_mapping.keys()}
    best_step_avg = -1
    best_step_str = ""

    for run in runs:
        try:
            summary_metrics = json.loads(run["summaryMetrics"])
            step = summary_metrics.get("_step", 0)
            current_avg = 0
            count = 0
            for notion_col, wandb_key in benchmark_mapping.items():
                if wandb_key in summary_metrics:
                    score = summary_metrics[wandb_key]
                    if score > best_scores[notion_col]:
                        best_scores[notion_col] = score
                    current_avg += score
                    count += 1
            if count > 0:
                current_avg /= count
                if current_avg > best_step_avg:
                    best_step_avg = current_avg
                    best_step_str = f"{step}({current_avg:.4f})"
        except (json.JSONDecodeError, TypeError):
            continue

    results[run_name] = {
        "scores": best_scores,
        "best_step": best_step_str,
    }

for run_name, data in results.items():
    properties = {
        "Run Name": {"title": [{"text": {"content": run_name}}]},
        "Best Step (Average)": {"rich_text": [{"text": {"content": data["best_step"]}}]}
    }
    for benchmark, score in data["scores"].items():
        if score != -1:
            properties[benchmark] = {"number": score}

    print(f"Adding page for {run_name}")
    # default_api.notion_API_create_a_database(
    #     parent=default_api.NotionApiCreateADatabaseParent(page_id="275c4171-366e-80b7-9a0d-ffb6a4dfb523", type="page_id"),
    #     title=[default_api.NotionApiCreateADatabaseTitle(text=default_api.NotionApiCreateADatabaseTitleText(content=run_name))],
    #     properties=properties
    # )
    # The above is wrong, I should be creating a page in a database, not a database.

    # Correct tool is notion_API_post_page
    # default_api.notion_API_post_page(
    #     parent=default_api.NotionApiPostPageParent(database_id="0a16773d-6317-4aa4-8709-7e155588b82a"),
    #     properties=properties
    # )


```

```python 
import json
from google.generativeai.notebook.lib import llm_function_invoker

default_api = llm_function_invoker.LLMFunctionInvoker()

# Load the W&B data from the file
with open("/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/e9AUyeypZtyjjHpo6aWhiT.json", "r") as f:
    wandb_data = json.load(f)

# The actual data is nested inside the JSON
wandb_runs = json.loads(json.loads(wandb_data["text"])['text'])["project"]["runs"]["edges"]

# Group runs by displayName
runs_by_name = {}
for run_edge in wandb_runs:
    run = run_edge["node"]
    display_name = run["displayName"]
    if display_name not in runs_by_name:
        runs_by_name[display_name] = []
    runs_by_name[display_name].append(run)

# Define the mapping from Notion column names to W&B metric keys
benchmark_mapping = {
    "CodeIO": "val-core/simulation__codeio/acc/mean@1",
    "HiTab": "val-core/table__hitab/acc/mean@1",
    "SuperGPQA": "val-core/stem__supergpqa/acc/mean@1",
    "LiveCodeBench": "val-core/codegen__livecodebench/acc/mean@1",
    "AIME (8x)": "val-core/math__aime_repeated_8x/acc/best@8/mean",
    "Ordering Puzzle": "val-core/logic__ordering_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "HumanEval": "val-core/codegen__humaneval/acc/mean@1",
    "Graph Logical": "val-core/logic__graph_logical_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "MultiHiertt": "val-core/table__multihier/acc/mean@1",
    "ArcAgI1": "val-core/simulation__arcagi1/acc/mean@1",
    "MBPP": "val-core/codegen__mbpp/acc/mean@1",
    "Zebra Puzzle": "val-core/logic__zebra_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1",
    "MATH": "val-core/math__math/acc/mean@1",
    "GPQA": "val-core/stem__gpqa/acc/mean@1",
    "AMC (4x)": "val-core/math__amc_repeated_4x/acc/best@4/mean",
}

results = {}

for run_name, runs in runs_by_name.items():
    best_scores = {bm: -1 for bm in benchmark_mapping.keys()}
    best_step_avg = -1
    best_step_str = ""

    for run in runs:
        try:
            summary_metrics = json.loads(run["summaryMetrics"])
            step = summary_metrics.get("_step", 0)
            current_avg = 0
            count = 0
            for notion_col, wandb_key in benchmark_mapping.items():
                if wandb_key in summary_metrics:
                    score = summary_metrics[wandb_key]
                    if score > best_scores[notion_col]:
                        best_scores[notion_col] = score
                    current_avg += score
                    count += 1
            if count > 0:
                current_avg /= count
                if current_avg > best_step_avg:
                    best_step_avg = current_avg
                    best_step_str = f"{step}({current_avg:.4f})"
        except (json.JSONDecodeError, TypeError):
            continue

    results[run_name] = {
        "scores": best_scores,
        "best_step": best_step_str,
    }

for run_name, data in results.items():
    properties = {
        "Run Name": {"title": [{"text": {"content": run_name}}]},
        "Best Step (Average)": {"rich_text": [{"text": {"content": data["best_step"]}}]}
    }
    for benchmark, score in data["scores"].items():
        if score != -1:
            properties[benchmark] = {"number": score}

    parent = {"type": "database_id", "database_id": "0a16773d-6317-4aa4-8709-7e155588b82a"}

    print(f"Adding page for {run_name}")
    default_api.notion_API_post_page(
        parent=parent,
        properties=properties
    )

print("Done.")
```

```python 
    "AMC (4x)": "val-core/math__amc_repeated_4x/acc/best@4/mean",
```
